Moisture content of concrete after 1 and 21 days
115
==PAGE:123==
B.1
New titration equipment: Setup, user manual and
method analysis of Metrohm 888 Titrando with Tiamo 2.5
Software
Purpose
Section for Materials and Durability at DTU Civil Engineering has bought new titration
equipment: Metrohm Titrando 888 titrator controlled by the software Tiamo (version 2.5).
The present report is the result of testing the equipment, with the purpose of creating a
DTU specific user manual and testing the general method for accuracy.
The accuracy is tested by titrating 0.1M NaCl (1, 5 and 10 mL) with 0.1M AgNO3.
The user manual ”DTU User Manual for Titration with 888 Titrando using Tiamo 2.5 Soft­
ware” is not appended in the end of this report and can be retrived by contacting DTU Civil
Engineering, Section for Materials and Durability (att: Kurt Kielsgaard Hansen). It will not
be further discussed here.
Equipment
The Titrando System
• 888 Titrando with an Ag titrode
• 801 Stirrer / Stand and stirring magnet
• Computer with Tiamo 2.5 Software
Other laboratory equipment
• Pipette, Thermo Fisher 1 mL.
• Weight, Sartorius CP22d weight.
• Glass beaker, 250 mL
• Volumetric flask 1000mL ± 3.5mL
Chemicals
• 0.100 M AgNO3
• 0.1 M NaCl
• Deminiralised water
Procedure
The procedure is divided into 3 main parts; preparation of 0.1M NaCl, preperation of 888
Titrando and performing titration.
Preperation of 0.1M NaCl
A solution of 0.1 M NaCl is made. The solutions is made of 5.84399 g NaCl with 1000 mL
deminiralised water measured using a volumetric flask, weight of 995.32 g.
Preperation of 888 Titrando
The prepration of the 888 Titrando is performed using the Tiamo 2.5 software as described
in the appended user manual.
116
==PAGE:124==
Performing titration
Titration is performed with 3 different volumes of 0.100M NaCl: 1, 5 and 10 mL. For each
sample volume, 8 tests are performed (the same number of tests as a typical titration for
chloride profile) and therefore 8 glass beakers are prepared with the number from 1 to 8.
A 1 mL pipette is used to insert the right volume of NaCl into each of the beakers.
Each beaker is then topped with demineralised water until 200 mL and a stirring magnet
is added. The authors found that a total volume of 200 mL worked best.
The titration is started and results are retrieved as described in the user manual appended
to this report.
Results and discussion
Test of pipette
The used pipette for the titration experiment is tested. The test is to measure the weight
of the assumed 1.0 mL dosage. The mean weight is 1.001313 g/mL with a standard
deviation of 0.004175 g/mL, which corresponds to a relative deviation of 0.42%. This is
under the used pipette specified deviation.
Titration
The titration experiment results are shown in table B.1. Given the chemical equation,
B.1, will 1 mL silver nitrate correspond to 1mL sodium chloride given that they have equal
molarity. The results show that there is a small positive offset in the use of sliver nitrate
compared to the amount of sodium chloride. This offset seems not to be constant. The
authors find the variance acceptable and will not take the offset into account because it is
estimated to be negligible.
AgNO3 (aq) + NaCl (aq) −−→AgCl (s) + NaNO3 (aq)
(B.1)
Table B.1: The used volume of 0.1M AgNO3 which corresponds to the equivalence point
determined by the titration equipment for different amounts of NaCl.
Amount of 0.100M NaCl
Volume of 0.1M AgNO3
1 mL
5 mL
10 mL
Mean [mL]
1.0192
5.0436
10.0072
SD [mL]
0.0068
0.0104
0.0364
Rel. SD [%]
0.669
0.364
0.205
Stirring rate
The authors found a balanced vortex in the 200 mL sample when the stirring rate in the
801 Stirrer was set at 6. The stirring rate can be altered according to user manual.
Conclusion
The titration equipment have acceptable variance.
117
==PAGE:125==
B.2
Moisture content of concrete after 1 and 21 days
Purpose
Present thesis investigates the effect of epoxy painting on concrete exposed to seawater
after 2 and 28 days. The concrete which is exposed after 2 days is epoxy painted after 1
day and the concrete which is exposed after 28 days is epoxy painted after 21 days. It is of
interest to determine the moisture content of the concrete at the time of epoxy application,
since the product suppliers determine a moisture content limit for their products.
This experiment determines the moisture content of a Ø100x200 mm cylinder after 1 and
21 days.
Equipment and Procedure
Concrete mixing
• Concrete mix design (FAC) according to section 4.2
• Mixing, vibrating and casting of 2 Ø100x200 cylinders according to appendix A.3
Curing
• Temperature controlled room at 20◦C
• Plastic wrap
• Duct tape
Crushing and drying
• TONY 3000 compression machine
• Scale
• Metal tray capable of holding at least 1000 g
• Ventilated oven capable of maintaining 105◦C
Procedure
Concrete mixing
Since it is only the FAC which has been epoxy painted, only this recipe is tested. Concrete
is mixed and vibrated according to appendix A.3. 2 cylinders is used.
Curing
The cylinder is cured in the mould for 24 hours in a temperature controlled room of 20◦C.
The concrete which has to be tested after 1 day is directly transfered from the mould to
next step. The concrete which has to be tested after 21 days is wrapped in plastic, sealed
tight with duct tape and left for curing in the temperature controlled room (20◦C)
Crushing and drying
After desired curing time, the cylinder is placed in the TONY 3000 testing machine and
’crushed’ as described in appendix A.9. However, instead of setting the fracture detection
(FRACT.DET) to 0.150%, it is now increased to 10% in order to make sure the concrete
is completely crushed.
Note the weight of the empty metal tray (mc). Immediately after crushing, at least 1000 g
of crushed concrete sample is placed in the metal tray and weighted (m). The tray with
concrete is placed in the ventilated oven which is set at 105◦C.
118
==PAGE:126==
The sample is maintained in the oven until and weighed regularly until a constant mass is
achieved. This weight is noted down (m0). Calcualte the moisture content in the sample
from
The moisture content is calculated from eq. (B.2).
u = m −m0
m0 −mc
· 100%
(B.2)
Where
u
is the moisture content, in %
m
is the mass of the aggregates and container before drying, in g.
m0
is the mass of the aggregates and container after drying, in g
mc
is the mass of the heat resistant container, in kg
Results and discussion
The results can be seen in table B.2.
Table B.2: Moisture content of a FAC after 1 and 21 days
1 MD
21 MD
Mass before drying, m [g]
1542.82
1167.41
Mass after drying, m0 [g]
1462.13
1123.29
Mass of container, mc [g]
29.02
28.88
Moisture content, u [%]
5.63
4.03
The found moisture content of 5.63% for a specimen cured for 1 day and 4.03% for 21
days is reasonable and the results can be used for discussion regarding the application
of epoxy coating.
Conclusion
The moisture content for specimen cured for 1 day was found to be 5.63% for and for 21
day this is 4.03%.

Explanation of calculations
Dnssm
: non-steady-state migration coefficient [m2/s]
z
: absolute value of ion valence, for chloride, z = 1
F
: Faraday constant, F = 9.648 x 104 [J/(V mol)]
U
: absolute value of the applied voltage [V]
R
: gas contant, R = 8.341 [J / (K mol)]
T
:
L
: thickness of the speciment [m]
xd
: average value of the penetration depths [m]
t
: test duration [s]
erf-1
: inverse of error function
cd
:
c0
:
average value of the initial and final temperatures in 
the anolyte solution [K]
chloride concentration at which the colour changes, 
cd ≈ 0.07 M for OPC concrete

Explanation for calculations
Symbols
The following equation numbers refer to the numbers showed above the columns of the first calculation
u
Water content [%]
m
Mass of sample and glass before drying [g]
m0
Mass of sample and glass after drying [g]
mc
Mass of glass [g]
mCl-
Mass of chlorides in solution [g]
V0.1M AgNO3
Volume of 0.1M AgNO3 titrant added to obtain EP [ml]
V0.1M NaCl
Volumen of 0.1 M NaCl added to sample prior to titration [ml]
MCl-
Molar mass of chloride ions (35.45 [g/mol])
Cmean
Measured mean concentration of interval [%]
Ccalc
Calculated mean concentration of interval [%]
Ci
Initial chloride concentration of concrete [%]
Cs
Surface concentration obtained by minimising error of GRG non-linear solve [%]
xmean
Mean distance to surface of interval [mm]
Dapp
Apparent diffusion coefficent obtained by minimising error GRG non-linear solve [m2/s]
t
The age of the concrete at end of exposure (curing + exposure) [days]

NOTE: Due to measurement uncertainties the values of Cmean sometimes is less than the theoretical possible Ci. Since this 
is of no physical meaning, the calculation with (Cmean-Ccalc)2 has an built in IF-statement, where IF(Cmean < Ci , (Ci-Ccalc)2 , 
(Cmean-Ccalc)2).
The calculation of Dapp and Cs is performed with the Excel add-in "Solver". The solver uses a GRG non-linear solve to 
minimise the sum of errors squared to find the optimal Dapp and Cs values. The values used for this solve is marked with 
blue fill.

E
Statistical analysis
Analysis of variance ­ Anova
Analysis of variance provides a statistical test of whether two or more population means
are equal. The calculations are performed using the software R. For more information
see general literature about statistical analysis and the use of R.
E.1
Apparent diffusion coefficients
E.1.1
FAC
# Create a sequence of numbers
X = data.frame(difFAC= c(8.428, 7.796, 9.096,
7.845, 8.993, 9.783,
7.277, 8.370, 6.575,
7.149, 5.576, 6.170,
4.676, 5.039, 5.280,
3.953, 3.470, 3.456),
age=
factor(c(1, 1, 1,
2, 2, 2,
4, 4, 4,
7, 7, 7,
14, 14, 14,
28, 28, 28)))
# Create a linear model called "fitFAC"
fitFAC <- lm(difFAC ~ age, data=X)
anovatestFAC <- anova(fitFAC)
# Display of Analysis of Variance Table
anovatestFAC
## Analysis of Variance Table
##
## Response: difFAC
##

Pr(>F)

par(mfrow=c(1,2))
#Check residuals, plot Q-Q plot
qqnorm(fitFAC$residuals)
qqline(fitFAC$residuals)
#Plot boxplot
plot(X$age, fitFAC$residuals,
xlab="Age of start of exposure in days", ylab="Residuals")

Assumptions regarding ANOVA seems acceptable.
M <- 6*(6-1)/2
alpha_bonferroni <- 0.05/M
LSD_alphaB <- qt(1-alpha_bonferroni/2, 18) *
sqrt(2*anovatestFAC$`Mean Sq`[2]/6)

# Create a sequence of numbers

Produkt datablad  
Udgave 22/01/2008 
 
Sikagard®-Wallcoat N 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
1 
1/6 
Construction 
 
Sikagard®-Wallcoat N 
2-komponent vanddispergeret epoxy maling 
Produkt 
beskrivelse 
Sikagard®-Wallcoat N er en 2-komponent, farvet, vanddispergeret epoxy. 
Anvendelsesområder 
 
Farvet coating til indendørs vægoverflader 
 
Til beton og cementbaserede overflader 
 
Velegnet til produktionsfaciliteter, lager og logistik områder etc. 
Egenskaber/fordele 
 
God kemisk og mekanisk resistens 
 
God vedhæftning til overflader med fugt 
 
God dækkeevne 
 
Vanddampdiffusionsåben 
 
Afgiver ikke dampe 
 
Karbonatiseringsbremsende 
 
Vandfortyndbar 
 
Nem påføring 
 
Kan sprøjtepåføres 
 
Nem at rengøre 
 
“Synker” ikke 
 
Lugtfri 
Tests 
 
Afprøvninger/ 
standarder 
Opfylder kravene til afgasning med klasse “Excellent” i henhold  
DIN 24415. 
Brand test i henhold til DIN 13505-1, class B1. 
Produkt Data 
 
Form 
 
Udseende / farve 
Resin - komp A: 
Farvet, flydende 
Hærder - komp B: 
Transparent, flydende 
Tilgængelige farver: Ca. RAL 9003, 9010, 7032, 7035 
Andre farver kan produceres. 
Ved direkte solpåvirkning  kan der forekomme misfarvninger og farve forskelle, dette 
har ingen indflydelse på malingens funktion og egenskaber. 
==PAGE:174==
 
 
2 
2/6 
Emballager 
Komp A: 
14,4 kg spande 
Komp B: 
  5,6 kg spande 
Komp A+B: 20 kg i færdigdoserede emballage 
Lager 
 
Lager konditioner / 
holdbarhed 
12 mdr. fra produktionsdato opbevaret i originale og uåbnede emballager, i tørre 
omgivelser og ved temperatur mellem +5°C og +30°C. 
Tekniske Data 
 
Kemisk base 
Epoxy, vand dispergeret 
Densitet 
Komp. A: 
~ 1,58 kg/l 
(DIN EN ISO 2811-1)
Komp. B: 
~ 1,07 kg/l 
Komp. A+B 
~ 1,39 kg/l 
Alle densitet værdier ved +23°C 
Tørstofindhold 
~ 50% ( volume) / ~  64% ( vægt ) 
Viskositet 
1030 mPas ved +23°C (komp. A+B) 
Mekaniske / Fysiske 
egenskaber 
 
Slidstyrke 
94 mg (CS 10/1000/1000) 
(14 dage / +23°C)  (DIN 53 109, Taber Abrader Test) 
Resistens 
 
Kemisk resistens 
Resistent over for mange kemikalier. Resistens tabel kan rekvireres. 
 
Påvirkning* 
Tør varme 
Permanent 
+50°C 
Kortvarigt max. 7 døgn 
+80°C 
Kortvarigt max. 12 timer 
+100°C 
Termisk resistens 
Kortvarigt  fugtig/våd varme op til +80°C hvor påvirkningen kun er en gang i mellem 
(højtryksspuling etc.) 
*ingen samtidig kemisk og mekanisk påvirkning. 
System 
Information 
 
System struktur 
Primer: 
På gipsplade vægge*:  
1 x Sikafloor®-156 + 20% Fortynder C 
På mørtler:  
1 x Sikafloor®-156 + 20% Fortynder C  
 
eller 1 x Sikagard-Wallcoat N + 5 % vand 
På beton:   
1 x Sikafloor®-156 + 20% Fortynder C  
 
eller 1 x Sikagard®-Wallcoat N + 5% vand 
Dæklag:  
2 - 3 x Sikagard®-Wallcoat N (rulle påføring) 
 
eller 1 - 2 x Sikagard®-Wallcoat N (sprøjtepåført) 
*  For påføring på gipsplader, referer venligst til  “Noter om 
påføring/begrænsninger”. 
==PAGE:175==
 
 
3 
3/6 
Udførelsesdetaljer 
 
 
Malings system 
Produkt 
Forbrug 
Primer 
Sikafloor®-156+ 20% Fortynder C eller 
Sikagard®-Wallcoat N + 5% vand 
~ 0,08 kg/m
2 
~ 0,15 – 0.20 kg/m
2

påføring)

2 pr 
påføring 
0,15 - 0,28 kg/m
2 pr 
påføring 
Forbrug og blanding 
Alle angivne mængder er teoretiske og inkluderer ikke merforbrug på grund af 
udførelsesteknik, porøse overflader, overfladens profil samt variationer i planhed og 
spild etc. 
Overfladens kvalitet 
Betonoverfladen skal være sund og have en tilstrækkelig trykstyrke (minimum 25 
N/mm2) med en minimum aftræksstyrke på 1,5 N/mm2. 
Overfladen skal være ren, tør og fri for alle forureninger såsom olie, fedt, coatninger 
og overfladebehandlinger etc. 
I tvivlstilfælde udføres et test areal. 
Forbehandling 
Betonoverladen skal slyngrenses eller fræses for at fjerne cementslam for at opnå 
en god struktur og opfylde CSP 3-6 i henhold The International Concrete Repair 
Institute. 
Svag beton skal fjernes og overfladedefekter som større huller og hulrum skal 
åbnes. 
Reparationer af disse defekter skal foretages med velegnede produkter fra 
Sikafloor, SikaDur og Sikagard produkterne. 
Høje områder kan fjernes ved slibning. 
Alt støv, løse partikler og materiale skal fjernes fuldstændig fra overfladen med kost 
og grundig støvsugning inden påføring . 
Betonen eller belægningsoverfladen skal primes eller spartles for at opnå en plan 
overflade. 
Alt støv, løse partikler og materiale skal fjernes fuldstændig fra overfladen med kost 
og grundig støvsugning inden påføring . 
Påføringskonditioner 
og begrænsninger 
 
Overflade temperatur 
+10°C min. / +30°C max. 
Lufttemperatur  
+10°C min. / +30°C max. 
Overfladefugtighed 
< 6% (vægt) fugtindhold.  
Test metode: Sika®-Tramex Måler, CM – måling eller veje/tørre-metode. 
Ingen opstigende fugt i henhold til ASTM (Polyethylen-folie test). 
Relativ  luftfugtighed 
75% RF max. 
Dugpunkt 
Vær opmærksom på kondens. 
Overfladen og det uhærdede materiale skal være mindst 3°C over dugpunktet for at 
reducere risikoen for kondens og defekter i belægningens finish. 
==PAGE:176==
 
 
4 
4/6 
Påførings- 
instruktioner 
 
Blanding 
Komp. A : Komp. B = 73 : 27 (vægt) ; 65:35 (volume) 
Blandetid 
Før sammenblanding, røres komponent A mekanisk. Når hele komponent B er 
hældt sammen med komponent A, blandes konstant i 3 minutter indtil der opnås en 
ensartet konsistens og farve. 
For at sikre en korrekt blanding af materialet omhældes blandingen til et andet 
blandekar og blandes igen til korrekt konsistens. 
Over-blanding skal undgåes for at minimere luftindblanding. 
Blandeudstyr 
Sikagard®-Wallcoat N skal blandes omhyggeligt med en langsomtgående elektrisk 
blander (300 - 400 omdr./min.) eller andet egnet udstyr. 
Påføringsmetode /  
værktøj 
Før påføring kontrolleres overfladens fugtindhold, den relative luftfugtighed og 
dugpunktet.  
Hvis > 6% (vægt) fugtindhold, påføres Sikagard-720 EpoCem, som et midlertidigt 
fugtbarriere system. 
Primer: 
Det skal sikres, at primeren danner en porefri behandling af overfladen. Påfør 
Sikafloor primeren pensel eller rulle.  
Vægmaling: 
Påfør Sikagard®-Wallcoat N med rulle. 
Sikagard®-Wallcoat N kan også påføres med airlessprøjte (sprøjtetryk ~ 300 bar, 
dyse med en diameter på 0,53 mm / 0,021 tomme og vinkel på 60°). 
Rengøring af værktøj 
Umiddelbart efter brug rengøres alt værktøj med rent vand.  Hærdet materiale kan 
kun fjernes mekanisk. 
 
Temperatur 
Tid 
+10°C 
~ 150 min. 
+20°C 
~ 90 min. 
+30°C 
~ 60 min. 
Potlife 
 
Før påføring af Sikagard®-Wallcoat N på Sikafloor®-156 ventes: 
Overfladetemperatur 
Minimum 
Maksimum 
+10°C 
24 timer 
4 dage 
+20°C 
12 timer 
2 dage 
+30°C 
6 timer 
1 dage 
 
Før påføring af Sikagard®-Wallcoat N på Sikagard®-Wallcoat N ventes: 
Overfladetemperatur 
Minimum 
Maksimum 
+10°C 
180 min. 
7 dage 
+20°C 
180 min. 
7 dage 
+30°C 
150 min. 
7 dage 
Ventetid/ overmalings- 
interval 
Alle tider er cirka og vil være afhængig af de omgivende konditioner og ændringer i 
disse - f.eks. temperatur og RF. 
==PAGE:177==
 
 
5 
5/6 
BEMÆRK ! 
Påføring/begræsninger 
Påfør ikke Sikagard®-Wallcoat N på overflader med opstigende fugt. 
Påfør ikke Sikagard®-Wallcoat N på gipsplader, hvis det er i våde rum, som f.eks. 
baderum etc. 
Nypåført Sikagard®-Wallcoat N skal beskyttes mod fugt, kondens og  vand i mindst 
24 timer. 
Ved påføring af Sikagard®-Wallcoat N i mindre områder/lokaler skal der etableres 
en god ventilation for at undgå hærdeproblemer. 
Forkert vurdering og behandling af revner kan medføre kortere genbehandlings 
interval og tilbagevendende revner. 
For at sikre korrekt farve match skal det sikres, at  Sikagard®-Wallcoat N i hvert 
område påføres fra samme batch. 
Ved sprøjtepåføring skal det korrekte sikkerheds- og beskyttelses udstyr anvendes! 
Hvis der kræves opvarmning bør der ikke anvendes gas, olie, petroleum eller 
paraffin brændere. Disse producerer store mængder af både CO2 og vanddamp, 
dette kan medføre skader i den endelige finish. Der bør altid anvendes elektrisk 
opvarmning.

MasterSeal M 338 
Vandbaseret epoxycoating til vandtætning og beskyttelse af betonelementer. 
Drikkevandsgodkendt 
 
Maj 2018 erst. aug 2013 
 
ANVENDELSESOMRÅDER 
• Til indendørs og udendørs brug 
• Egnet til vandrette og lodrette overflader 
• Kan anvendes på beton og cementmørtel 
• Til beskyttelse af rør, kanaler, tanke, afløb osv. 
• Til brug på støttevægge, brodæk og bygningskonstrukti-
oner mm.  
• Til beskyttelse af tunneler 
For alle anvendelser, som ikke er nævnt her, kontakt den 
tekniske serviceafdeling hos BASF. 
 
EGENSKABER OG FORDELE 
• Vandbaseret, miljøvenligt 
• Fremragende vedhæftning på beton, også fugtig beton 
• Er materialet først hærdet, er det diffusionstæt for vand 
og kuldioxid 
• Ikke antændeligt 
• God gennemtrængelighed for vanddamp - lav risiko for 
blæredannelse 
• Modstandsdygtigt over for vand, vejr og frost 
• God kemisk resistens (se skema) 
• Høj slidstyrke 
• Nem rengøring og vedligeholdelse 
• Drikkevandsgodkendt 
• Lav brandklasse (klasse Bfl-s1) 
 
MATERIALEBASIS 
To-komponent vandbaseret epoxycoating. Indeholder ikke 
opløsningsmidler 
 
FORARBEJDNING 
(a) Forhandling af underlag: 
Alle underlag (gamle og nye) skal være faste og bæredyg-
tige, tørre og fri for cementslam og løstsiddende partikler 
samt fri for olie, fedt, gummimærker, malingrester og an-
dre vedhæftningshindrende forureninger. Overfladen bør 
forbehandles ved hjælp af sandblæsning, højtryksrensning 
eller en anden passende mekanisk behandling. 
 
Underlagets temperatur bør være mindst +10 °C og maks. 
+30 °C. 
 
Efter forberedelse af overfladen skal underlagets sam-
menhængsstyrke være større end 1,5 N/mm2 (kontrolleres 
vha. et godkendt aftræksapparat). 
 
 
Restfugtigheden i underlaget må ikke være højere end 8 
% (kontrolleres fx vha. CM-apparat). Underlagets tempe-
ratur skal være mindst 3 °C over den aktuelle dugpunkt-
temperatur. Temperaturen bør under påføring og hærd-
ning holdes så konstant som muligt. 
 
(b) Blanding: 
MasterSeal M 338 leveres som to separate komponenter, 
afstemt i et korrekt blandingsforhold klar til brug. 
 
Komponent B hældes i komponent A. Sørg for, at embal-
lagen med komponent B tømmes fuldstændigt. Herefter 
blandes med egnet røre- eller blandeværktøj påsat en 
langsomtgående boremaskine (ca. 400 o/min), indtil der er 
opnået en homogen blanding. 
 
Undgå, at der kommer luft i blandingen. Delvis blanding er 
strengt forbudt. 
 
(c) Påføring: 
MasterSeal M 338 påføres normalt i to eller tre lag. For-
bruget pr. lag afhænger af underlagets ruhed og påfø-
ringsmetoden. 
 
il første lag fortyndes materialet med 10 % rent lednings-
vand. De efterfølgende lag skal påføres ufortyndet, når det 
første lag er klæbefrit. 
 
MasterSeal M 338 kan påføres med pensel, kortluvet rulle 
eller airless-sprøjtepistol. 
 
RENGØRING AF VÆRKTØJ 
Værktøj kan rengøres med vand, så længe materialet ikke 
er hærdet. Er materialet først hærdet, kan det kun fjernes 
mekanisk. 
 
FORBRUG 
Der skal mindst påføres to lag. Første lag påføres med et 
forbrug på ca. 0,20 kg pr. m2. Det næste og de efterføl-
gende lag kræver ca. 0,25 - 0,30 kg/m2 pr. lag. Disse 
forbrugsværdier er teoretiske værdier og kan variere alt 
efter underlagets sugeevne og ruhed. Det er vigtigt at 
gennemføre forsøg på byggepladsen til vurdering af det 
nøjagtige forbrug.

andre stoffer, der kan påvirke materialets egenskaber.

DESCRIPTION OF THE PRODUCT
Dynamon XTend 200 is an efficient superplasticising 
admixture for concrete which gives the concrete long 
workability. The product combines the high water 
reducing effect from the Dynamon-product range with 
a new type of polymers that is gradually activated over 
time to maintain the concrete’s workability. 
Dynamon XTend 200 is specially developed for 
cements from Alborg Portland, but will also work well in 
other cements.
WHERE TO USE
Dynamon XTend 200 is used to get a high workability 
and very low loss of consistency.
Some special areas of use are:
• self-compacting concrete (SCC) with high slump 
retention requirements;
• production of frost resistant concrete with high 
demands to air void structure – in combination with 
Mapeair air entraining admixture;
• concretes with special requirements: high slump 
retention, high strength, low permeability, durability in 
aggressive environments.
Concretes containing Dynamon XTend 200 will 
normally not need extra addition on site, although this is 
possible with Dynamon XTend 200.
TECHNICAL CHARACTERISTICS
Dynamon XTend 200 combines the latest generation 
active acrylic polymers which very efficiently disperse 
the cement particles, thus reducing the inner friction 
in the concrete. In addition Mapei has in their research 
department developed a new type of polymer that 
retains the concrete’s workability for a long time without 
influencing early strength development for the concrete.
DOSAGE
To obtain the required properties (workability, strength, 
impermeability, durability, etc.), Dynamon XTend 200 is 
added in dosages between 0.3 and 2.0 % by weight of 
cement. Higher dosages increase the slump retention. 
Higher dosages and lower concrete temperatures also 
slow down the hydration process. 
Dynamon XTend 200 is added after all the other 
ingredients (water, cement and aggregates) are added 
in the mixer.
Dynamon XTend 200 can also be added directly into a 
truck mixer. The mixing time is then 1 minute pr m³ at 
maximum rotation speed, though never shorter than 5 
minutes.
COMPATIBILITY WITH OTHER ADMIXTURES
Dynamon XTend 200 can be combined with other 
admixtures from Mapei: such as Mapefast set and 
hardening accelerators.
The product is also compatible with Mapeair air 
entraining agents. The choice of admixture is done after 
an evaluation of the properties of the other ingredients 
in the mix.
PACKAGING
Dynamon XTend 200 is available in 25 liter cans, 200 
liter barrels, 1000 liter containers and in bulk.

but this will not affect the technical properties 
of the product.

WHERE TO USE
Anti-adhesive treatment of iron, aluminum and 
plastic forms (epoxy, phenolic, polyester and 
polyurethane resins). 
Some application examples
• To facilitate form release of precast concrete.
• To facilitate form release of steam-cured 
concrete.
• To form release concrete cast in plastic forms.
• To form release concrete cast in metal forms.
TECHNICAL CHARACTERISTICS
Mapeform Eco Oil 700 consists of a stable 
mixture of selected vegetable oils, corrosion 
inhibitors and special admixtures developed in the 
MAPEI research laboratories.
The efficiency of Mapeform Eco Oil 700 is given 
by its action of chemical concrete stripping from 
formwork.
Mapeform Eco Oil 700 features the following 
advantages:
• improved surface quality thanks to the drastic 
reduction of large and micro surface air bubbles;
• less cleaning of forms;
• simple low-cost application;
• easily and rapidly biodegradable; non 
toxic, it does not irritate and does not cause 
sensitization;
• not subject to the Italian law 303 of 1956 for the 
use of form release-agents based on mineral 
oils.
RECOMMENDATIONS
• Do not dilute Mapeform Eco Oil 700 with water.
• Do not dilute Mapeform Eco Oil 700 with 
solvents or other oils.
• Preferably use Mapeform-range with raw wood 
forms.
• Do not use Mapeform Eco Oil 700 with 
concrete, gypsum or polystyrene forms.
• When using with rubber forms make sample 
tests or contact the MAPEI Technical Services 
Department.
DIRECTIONS FOR USE
Mapeform Eco Oil 700 is ready-to-use.
Application
Apply Mapeform Eco Oil 700 on the clean, 
dry formwork, preferably in a single coat, using 
pressure pumps fitted with a misting nozzle or 
atomisers at a pressure of 6 Bar.
For effective stripping of forms, do not exceed 
the recommended dosage. This can cause the 
formation of a fine dust on the surface which can 
alter the final finish.
Cleaning
Tools used for applying Mapeform Eco Oil 700 
can be cleaned with water.
CONSUMPTION
Metal forms: 15-25 g/m².
Plastic forms: 15-25 g/m².
Form release agent 
based on vegetable oils 
at low viscosity
